Comment: hey_laughing_boy said "This that face you make when you too lazy to reach for the remote..
I remember this one time I was with my boy @tnol24 and we was out having a good day applying for a new job because the one we had almost had us out on the streets, and I'm not talking about being homeless.. Anyways everything going good I got the application and all filled it out waited about two weeks.. I go back to Tyler place about that time period and we wanna have a good day so Tyler takes me out to lake Whitney talking about he got a boat and it'll be a good time... It was a windy day if memory serves correctly, windy enough to blow the sense out of Tyler brain.. by the time we got to the lake and had the boat in the water we ran out of Gas I ain't ever seen disappointment on anyone's fathers face like I did that day.. Felt like I was a witness to a crime scene.. Tyler dad had that look in his eye that a father gives when they finally ready for a paternity test.. I can still feel the wind at my back when I went and borrowed a tube to syphon gas out the boat for the truck.. Had me trekking to the nearest RV for a Good Samaritan.. I found one and I swear he had shorts shorter than Tyler memory.. Luckily we never had to use that tube because Tyler dad went and got us some gas.. I can understand why he was mad that day.. Anyways moral of the story is don't be so lazy that you neglect your gas tank.. ğŸ˜‚ğŸ˜‚ğŸ˜‚"

Comment: hey_laughing_boy said "This that face you make when you too lazy to reach for the remote..
I remember this one time I was with my boy @tnol24 and we was out having a good day applying for a new job because the one we had almost had us out on the streets, and I'm not talking about being homeless.. Anyways everything going good I got the application and all filled it out waited about two weeks.. I go back to Tyler place about that time period and we wanna have a good day so Tyler takes me out to lake Whitney talking about he got a boat and it'll be a good time... It was a windy day if memory serves correctly, windy enough to blow the sense out of Tyler brain.. by the time we got to the lake and had the boat in the water we ran out of Gas I ain't ever seen disappointment on anyone's fathers face like I did that day.. Felt like I was a witness to a crime scene.. Tyler dad had that look in his eye that a father gives when they finally ready for a paternity test.. I can still feel the wind at my back when I went and borrowed a tube to syphon gas out the boat for the truck.. Had me trekking to the nearest RV for a Good Samaritan.. I found one and I swear he had shorts shorter than Tyler memory.. Luckily we never had to use that tube because Tyler dad went and got us some gas.. I can understand why he was mad that day.. Anyways moral of the story is don't be so lazy that you neglect your gas tank.. ğŸ˜‚ğŸ˜‚ğŸ˜‚"
